    window.addEventListener('message', function (event) {
          function getCookie(name) {
            var matches = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(
              "(?:^|; )" + name + "=([^;]*)"
            ))
            return matches && matches[1]
          }

          if(false) {
            var overlay = document.querySelector('.truste_overlay');
            var body = document.querySelector('body');

            if (overlay) {
              overlay.style.display = 'none';
            }
          }

          function isSubmitPrefMessage(messageObj) {
            return messageObj.source === 'preference_manager'
              && messageObj.message === 'submit_preferences'
          }

          function includes(str, searchString) {
            return typeof str === 'string'
              ? (str || '').indexOf(searchString) !== -1
              : null
          }

          // filter out messages from different origins
          if (!includes(event.origin, 'consent-pref.trustarc.com')) return

          try {
            var messageObj = JSON.parse(event.data)
          } catch (err) {
            console.error(err.message)
          }

          if (!isSubmitPrefMessage(messageObj)) return

          var isAnalyticsCurrAllowed =
            includes(messageObj.data, '2')

          var prefCookie = getCookie('notice_gdpr_prefs')

          // first time visitor (no cookie) and accepted analytics cookies
          if (!prefCookie && isAnalyticsCurrAllowed) return

          var isAnalyticsPrevAllowed = includes(prefCookie, '2')

          // take actions only when cookie preferences changed
          // and it's not the first visit (cookie exists)
          if (!!prefCookie && isAnalyticsPrevAllowed === isAnalyticsCurrAllowed) return

          if (!isAnalyticsCurrAllowed) {
            document.cookie = 'ab-cid= ; expires = Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT'
          }

          location.reload(true)
        })
